       940 +        bindEvents() {                                       
       941 +            let lastKey = null;                              
       942 +                                                             
       943 +            document.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {    
       944 +                // ењљзХ•иЊУеЕ•ж°ЖдЄ≠зЪДжМЙйФЃ                        
       945 +                if (e.target.matches('input, textarea')) retu
           +rn;                                                          
       946 +                                                             
       947 +                const key = e.key.toLowerCase();             
       948 +                                                             
       949 +                // жШЊз§ЇеЄЃеК©                                  
       950 +                if (e.shiftKey && key === '?') {             
       951 +                    e.preventDefault();                      
       952 +                    this.showHelp();                         
       953 +                    return;                                  
       954 +                }                                            
       955 +                                                             
       956 +                // жРЬзіҐ                                      
       957 +                if (key === '/' && !e.shiftKey) {            
       958 +                    e.preventDefault();                      
       959 +                    const searchInput = document.getElementBy
           +Id('searchInput');                                           
       960 +                    if (searchInput) {                       
       961 +                        searchInput.focus();                 
       962 +                    }                                        
       963 +                    return;                                  
       964 +                }                                            
       965 +                                                             
       966 +                // GG - ињФеЫЮй°ґйГ®                             
       967 +                if (key === 'g' && lastKey === 'g') {        
       968 +                    e.preventDefault();                      
       969 +                    window.scrollTo({ top: 0, behavior: 'smoo
           +th' });                                                      
       970 +                    return;                                  
       971 +                }                                            
       972 +                                                             
       973 +                // Shift+G - жїЪеК®еИ∞еЇХйГ®                      
       974 +                if (key === 'g' && e.shiftKey) {             
       975 +                    e.preventDefault();                      
       976 +                    window.scrollTo({ top: document.body.scro
           +llHeight, behavior: 'smooth' });                             
       977 +                    return;                                  
       978 +                }                                            
       979 +                                                             
       980 +                lastKey = key;                               
       981 +                setTimeout(() => { lastKey = null; }, 500);  
       982 +            });                                              
       983 +        },                                                   
       984 +
